Gold and elixir can be used to build and reload defenses that protect the player from other players’ attacks. Gems are the premium currency that helps to speed constructions or substitute other currency. \r\n\r\nThe game also features two single player campaign in which the player can attack a series of fortified enemy castles and earn gold and elixir.
